Python Code python
import os import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re from datetime import datetime print('=== DETAILED ANALYSIS OF COLLECTED JERRY YANG DOCUMENTARY MATERIALS ===') print('Analyzing saved HTML files and research data to identify documentary connections') print('Target: Jerry Yang appearances, We Live in Public connections, Sundance winners') print('=' * 90) # First, inspect the existing research results file structure results_file = 'workspace/jerry_yang_documentary_research.json' if os.path.exists(results_file): print('Found existing research results file. Inspecting structure...') with open(results_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: research_data = json.load(f) print('Research data structure:') print(f'Keys in data: {list(research_data.keys())}') print(f'Search timestamp: {research_data.get("timestamp", "N/A")}') print(f'Total findings: {len(research_data.get("all_findings", []))}') print(f'Documentary candidates: {len(research_data.get("documentary_candidates", []))}') print(f'Search methods: {len(research_data.get("search_methods", []))}') if research_data.get('all_findings'): print(f'\nFirst finding structure:') first_finding = research_data['all_findings'][0] print(f'Keys in finding: {list(first_finding.keys())}') else: print('No existing research results found.') research_data = {'all_findings': [], 'documentary_candidates': []} print('\n' + '=' * 90) print('ANALYZING SAVED HTML FILES FOR DOCUMENTARY CONNECTIONS') print('=' * 90) # List all HTML files in workspace html_files = [f for f in os.listdir('workspace') if f.endswith('.html')] print(f'Found {len(html_files)} HTML files to analyze:') for file in html_files: print(f' - {file}') # Initialize detailed analysis results detailed_analysis = { 'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'files_analyzed': [], 'jerry_yang_references': [], 'documentary_connections': [], 'we_live_in_public_analysis': {}, 'sundance_connections': [], 'ondi_timoner_filmography': [], 'key_findings': [] } # Analyze each HTML file in detail for html_file in html_files: print(f'\n=== ANALYZING {html_file.upper()} ===') print('-' * 60) file_path = os.path.join('workspace', html_file) file_analysis = { 'filename': html_file, 'file_size': os.path.getsize(file_path), 'jerry_yang_mentions': 0, 'documentary_mentions': 0, 'key_content': [], 'relevant_sections': [] } try: with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: html_content = f.read() soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') # Remove script and style elements for script in soup(["script", "style"]): script.decompose() # Get clean text text_content = soup.get_text() text_lower = text_content.lower() print(f'File size: {file_analysis["file_size"]:,} bytes') print(f'Text length: {len(text_content):,} characters') # Count key term mentions jerry_yang_count = text_lower.count('jerry yang') yang_count = text_lower.count('yang') - jerry_yang_count # Subtract to avoid double counting documentary_count = text_lower.count('documentary') film_count = text_lower.count('film') yahoo_count = text_lower.count('yahoo') file_analysis['jerry_yang_mentions'] = jerry_yang_count file_analysis['documentary_mentions'] = documentary_count print(f'Key term counts:') print(f' - "Jerry Yang": {jerry_yang_count}') print(f' - "Yang" (other): {yang_count}') print(f' - "Documentary": {documentary_count}') print(f' - "Film": {film_count}') print(f' - "Yahoo": {yahoo_count}') # Specific analysis based on file type if 'jerry_yang' in html_file: print('\n🎯 JERRY YANG PAGE ANALYSIS:') # Look for career section and media appearances career_section = soup.find(['h2', 'h3'], string=re.compile(r'Career|Biography|Life', re.IGNORECASE)) if career_section: print(' Found Career/Biography section') # Get content after career section next_content = career_section.find_next_sibling() while next_content and next_content.name not in ['h1', 'h2', 'h3']: content_text = next_content.get_text().strip() if len(content_text) > 50: content_lower = content_text.lower() if any(term in content_lower for term in ['documentary', 'film', 'interview', 'appeared', 'featured']): print(f' 📽️ Media reference: {content_text[:200]}...') file_analysis['key_content'].append(content_text[:300]) detailed_analysis['jerry_yang_references'].append({ 'source': 'Jerry Yang Wikipedia', 'content': content_text[:300], 'type': 'media_reference' }) next_content = next_content.find_next_sibling() # Look for any filmography or media sections media_sections = soup.find_all(['h2', 'h3', 'h4'], string=re.compile(r'Media|Film|Documentary|Interview|Appearance', re.IGNORECASE)) for section in media_sections: print(f' Found media section: {section.get_text()}') file_analysis['relevant_sections'].append(section.get_text()) elif 'we_live_in_public' in html_file: print('\n🎬 WE LIVE IN PUBLIC ANALYSIS:') # Look for cast, participants, or subject information cast_keywords = ['cast', 'participants', 'subjects', 'featuring', 'interviews'] for keyword in cast_keywords: cast_section = soup.find(['span', 'h2', 'h3'], string=re.compile(keyword, re.IGNORECASE)) if cast_section: print(f' Found {keyword} section') # Get content after this section next_element = cast_section.find_parent() if next_element: next_content = next_element.find_next_sibling() if next_content: cast_text = next_content.get_text() print(f' Content preview: {cast_text[:200]}...') # Check for Yahoo or Yang references cast_lower = cast_text.lower() if 'yahoo' in cast_lower or 'yang' in cast_lower: print(' ⭐ YAHOO/YANG CONNECTION FOUND!') detailed_analysis['we_live_in_public_analysis']['yahoo_connection'] = cast_text[:500] detailed_analysis['key_findings'].append({ 'type': 'yahoo_connection', 'source': 'We Live in Public', 'details': cast_text[:300] }) # Look for production information and awards awards_section = soup.find(['h2', 'h3'], string=re.compile(r'Awards|Reception|Festival', re.IGNORECASE)) if awards_section: print(' Found Awards/Festival section') awards_content = awards_section.find_next_sibling() if awards_content: awards_text = awards_content.get_text() print(f' Awards info: {awards_text[:200]}...') if 'sundance' in awards_text.lower(): print(' 🏆 SUNDANCE CONNECTION CONFIRMED!') detailed_analysis['sundance_connections'].append({ 'film': 'We Live in Public', 'award_info': awards_text[:300] }) elif 'ondi_timoner' in html_file: print('\n🎥 ONDI TIMONER FILMOGRAPHY ANALYSIS:') # Look for filmography section filmography_section = soup.find(['h2', 'h3'], string=re.compile(r'Filmography|Films|Work|Career', re.IGNORECASE)) if filmography_section: print(' Found Filmography section') # Extract film list next_element = filmography_section.find_next_sibling() while next_element and next_element.name not in ['h1', 'h2']: if next_element.name in ['ul', 'ol']: films = next_element.find_all('li') for film in films: film_text = film.get_text().strip() if len(film_text) > 10: print(f' Film: {film_text}') # Check for Yahoo or tech connections film_lower = film_text.lower() if any(term in film_lower for term in ['yahoo', 'internet', 'tech', 'digital', 'online']): print(f' 🔍 Tech connection: {film_text}') detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography'].append({ 'title': film_text, 'tech_connection': True }) else: detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography'].append({ 'title': film_text, 'tech_connection': False }) next_element = next_element.find_next_sibling() elif 'imdb' in html_file: print('\n🎭 IMDB SEARCH RESULTS ANALYSIS:') # Look for search results result_elements = soup.find_all(['td', 'div', 'li'], class_=lambda x: x and any(term in str(x).lower() for term in ['result', 'title', 'findResult'])) print(f' Found {len(result_elements)} potential result elements') for i, element in enumerate(result_elements[:10], 1): element_text = element.get_text().strip() if len(element_text) > 20 and len(element_text) < 500: print(f' Result {i}: {element_text[:150]}...') element_lower = element_text.lower() if any(term in element_lower for term in ['jerry yang', 'yahoo', 'documentary']): print(f' ⭐ Relevant result found!') file_analysis['key_content'].append(element_text) detailed_analysis['files_analyzed'].append(file_analysis) except Exception as e: print(f'Error analyzing {html_file}: {str(e)}') continue print(f'Analysis complete for {html_file}') # Generate comprehensive summary print('\n' + '=' * 90) print('COMPREHENSIVE DOCUMENTARY CONNECTION ANALYSIS') print('=' * 90) print(f'\n📊 ANALYSIS SUMMARY:') print(f'Files analyzed: {len(detailed_analysis["files_analyzed"])}') print(f'Jerry Yang references found: {len(detailed_analysis["jerry_yang_references"])}') print(f'Documentary connections: {len(detailed_analysis["documentary_connections"])}') print(f'Sundance connections: {len(detailed_analysis["sundance_connections"])}') print(f'Ondi Timoner films cataloged: {len(detailed_analysis["ondi_timoner_filmography"])}') print(f'Key findings: {len(detailed_analysis["key_findings"])}') # Display key findings if detailed_analysis['key_findings']: print('\n🎯 KEY FINDINGS:') for i, finding in enumerate(detailed_analysis['key_findings'], 1): print(f'\n{i}. Type: {finding["type"]}') print(f' Source: {finding["source"]}') print(f' Details: {finding["details"][:200]}...') else: print('\n❌ No key documentary connections identified') # Analyze We Live in Public specifically if detailed_analysis['we_live_in_public_analysis']: print('\n🎬 WE LIVE IN PUBLIC DETAILED ANALYSIS:') for key, value in detailed_analysis['we_live_in_public_analysis'].items(): print(f' {key}: {value[:200]}...') else: print('\n🎬 No specific We Live in Public connections found') # Display Ondi Timoner filmography if detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography']: print('\n🎥 ONDI TIMONER FILMOGRAPHY:') tech_films = [f for f in detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography'] if f.get('tech_connection')] other_films = [f for f in detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography'] if not f.get('tech_connection')] if tech_films: print(f' Tech-related films ({len(tech_films)}):'): for film in tech_films: print(f' - {film["title"]}') if other_films: print(f' Other films ({len(other_films)}):'): for film in other_films[:5]: # Show first 5 print(f' - {film["title"]}') if len(other_films) > 5: print(f' ... and {len(other_films) - 5} more films') # Save detailed analysis analysis_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'jerry_yang_detailed_documentary_analysis.json') with open(analysis_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(detailed_analysis, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\n💾 DETAILED ANALYSIS SAVED TO: {analysis_file}') # Create final summary report summary_report = f""" 🎯 JERRY YANG DOCUMENTARY CONNECTION RESEARCH - FINAL REPORT RESEARCH OBJECTIVE: Identify Jerry Yang's appearances in documentaries, particularly connections to 'We Live in Public', Josh Harris, and Sundance Grand Jury Prize winners. METHODS USED: 1. Wikipedia page analysis (Jerry Yang, We Live in Public, Ondi Timoner) 2. IMDb search result analysis 3. Direct HTML content parsing and keyword extraction 4. Comprehensive text analysis for documentary references KEY FINDINGS: - Files analyzed: {len(detailed_analysis['files_analyzed'])} - Jerry Yang documentary references: {len(detailed_analysis['jerry_yang_references'])} - We Live in Public connections: {'Found' if detailed_analysis['we_live_in_public_analysis'] else 'None confirmed'} - Sundance connections: {len(detailed_analysis['sundance_connections'])} - Ondi Timoner films cataloged: {len(detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography'])} CONCLUSIONS: {'Specific documentary connections identified' if detailed_analysis['key_findings'] else 'No direct Jerry Yang documentary appearances confirmed through available sources'} RECOMMENDATIONS: 1. Review saved HTML files manually for missed connections 2. Search academic databases for tech documentary histories 3. Contact documentary filmmakers directly for cast/participant information 4. Check video streaming platforms for documentary credits Analysis completed: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')} """ print(summary_report) # Save summary report summary_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'jerry_yang_documentary_final_report.txt') with open(summary_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(summary_report) print(f'\n📄 FINAL SUMMARY REPORT SAVED TO: {summary_file}') print('\n🏁 COMPREHENSIVE JERRY YANG DOCUMENTARY ANALYSIS COMPLETE!') print('All source materials analyzed and findings documented for further research.')

METHODS USED: 1. Wikipedia page analysis (Jerry Yang, We Live in Public, Ondi Timoner) 2. IMDb search result analysis 3. Direct HTML content parsing and keyword extraction 4. Comprehensive text analysis for documentary references KEY FINDINGS: - Files analyzed: {len(detailed_analysis['files_analyzed'])} - Jerry Yang documentary references: {len(detailed_analysis['jerry_yang_references'])} - We Live in Public connections: {'Found' if detailed_analysis['we_live_in_public_analysis'] else 'None confirmed'} - Sundance connections: {len(detailed_analysis['sundance_connections'])} - Ondi Timoner films cataloged: {len(detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography'])} CONCLUSIONS: {'Specific documentary connections identified' if detailed_analysis['key_findings'] else 'No direct Jerry Yang documentary appearances confirmed through available sources'} RECOMMENDATIONS: 1. Review saved HTML files manually for missed connections 2. Search academic databases for tech documentary histories 3. Contact documentary filmmakers directly for cast/participant information 4. Check video streaming platforms for documentary credits Analysis completed: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')} """ print(summary_report) # Save summary report summary_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'jerry_yang_documentary_final_report.txt') with open(summary_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(summary_report) print(f'\n📄 FINAL SUMMARY REPORT SAVED TO: {summary_file}') print('\n🏁 COMPREHENSIVE JERRY YANG DOCUMENTARY ANALYSIS COMPLETE!') print('All source materials analyzed and findings documented for further research.')

Python Code python
import os import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re from datetime import datetime print('=== DETAILED ANALYSIS OF COLLECTED JERRY YANG DOCUMENTARY MATERIALS ===') print('Analyzing saved HTML files and research data to identify documentary connections') print('Target: Jerry Yang appearances, We Live in Public connections, Sundance winners') print('=' * 90) # First, inspect the existing research results file structure results_file = 'workspace/jerry_yang_documentary_research.json' if os.path.exists(results_file): print('Found existing research results file. Inspecting structure...') with open(results_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: research_data = json.load(f) print('Research data structure:') print(f'Keys in data: {list(research_data.keys())}') print(f'Search timestamp: {research_data.get("timestamp", "N/A")}') print(f'Total findings: {len(research_data.get("all_findings", []))}') print(f'Documentary candidates: {len(research_data.get("documentary_candidates", []))}') print(f'Search methods: {len(research_data.get("search_methods", []))}') if research_data.get('all_findings'): print(f'\nFirst finding structure:') first_finding = research_data['all_findings'][0] print(f'Keys in finding: {list(first_finding.keys())}') else: print('No existing research results found.') research_data = {'all_findings': [], 'documentary_candidates': []} print('\n' + '=' * 90) print('ANALYZING SAVED HTML FILES FOR DOCUMENTARY CONNECTIONS') print('=' * 90) # List all HTML files in workspace html_files = [f for f in os.listdir('workspace') if f.endswith('.html')] print(f'Found {len(html_files)} HTML files to analyze:') for file in html_files: print(f' - {file}') # Initialize detailed analysis results detailed_analysis = { 'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'files_analyzed': [], 'jerry_yang_references': [], 'documentary_connections': [], 'we_live_in_public_analysis': {}, 'sundance_connections': [], 'ondi_timoner_filmography': [], 'key_findings': [] } # Analyze each HTML file in detail for html_file in html_files: print(f'\n=== ANALYZING {html_file.upper()} ===') print('-' * 60) file_path = os.path.join('workspace', html_file) file_analysis = { 'filename': html_file, 'file_size': os.path.getsize(file_path), 'jerry_yang_mentions': 0, 'documentary_mentions': 0, 'key_content': [], 'relevant_sections': [] } try: with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: html_content = f.read() soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') # Remove script and style elements for script in soup(["script", "style"]): script.decompose() # Get clean text text_content = soup.get_text() text_lower = text_content.lower() print(f'File size: {file_analysis["file_size"]:,} bytes') print(f'Text length: {len(text_content):,} characters') # Count key term mentions jerry_yang_count = text_lower.count('jerry yang') yang_count = text_lower.count('yang') - jerry_yang_count # Subtract to avoid double counting documentary_count = text_lower.count('documentary') film_count = text_lower.count('film') yahoo_count = text_lower.count('yahoo') file_analysis['jerry_yang_mentions'] = jerry_yang_count file_analysis['documentary_mentions'] = documentary_count print(f'Key term counts:') print(f' - "Jerry Yang": {jerry_yang_count}') print(f' - "Yang" (other): {yang_count}') print(f' - "Documentary": {documentary_count}') print(f' - "Film": {film_count}') print(f' - "Yahoo": {yahoo_count}') # Specific analysis based on file type if 'jerry_yang' in html_file: print('\n🎯 JERRY YANG PAGE ANALYSIS:') # Look for career section and media appearances career_section = soup.find(['h2', 'h3'], string=re.compile(r'Career|Biography|Life', re.IGNORECASE)) if career_section: print(' Found Career/Biography section') # Get content after career section next_content = career_section.find_next_sibling() while next_content and next_content.name not in ['h1', 'h2', 'h3']: if next_content.get_text: content_text = next_content.get_text().strip() if len(content_text) > 50: content_lower = content_text.lower() if any(term in content_lower for term in ['documentary', 'film', 'interview', 'appeared', 'featured']): print(f' 📽️ Media reference: {content_text[:200]}...') file_analysis['key_content'].append(content_text[:300]) detailed_analysis['jerry_yang_references'].append({ 'source': 'Jerry Yang Wikipedia', 'content': content_text[:300], 'type': 'media_reference' }) next_content = next_content.find_next_sibling() # Look for any filmography or media sections media_sections = soup.find_all(['h2', 'h3', 'h4'], string=re.compile(r'Media|Film|Documentary|Interview|Appearance', re.IGNORECASE)) for section in media_sections: print(f' Found media section: {section.get_text()}') file_analysis['relevant_sections'].append(section.get_text()) elif 'we_live_in_public' in html_file: print('\n🎬 WE LIVE IN PUBLIC ANALYSIS:') # Look for cast, participants, or subject information cast_keywords = ['cast', 'participants', 'subjects', 'featuring', 'interviews'] for keyword in cast_keywords: cast_section = soup.find(['span', 'h2', 'h3'], string=re.compile(keyword, re.IGNORECASE)) if cast_section: print(f' Found {keyword} section') # Get content after this section next_element = cast_section.find_parent() if next_element: next_content = next_element.find_next_sibling() if next_content: cast_text = next_content.get_text() print(f' Content preview: {cast_text[:200]}...') # Check for Yahoo or Yang references cast_lower = cast_text.lower() if 'yahoo' in cast_lower or 'yang' in cast_lower: print(' ⭐ YAHOO/YANG CONNECTION FOUND!') detailed_analysis['we_live_in_public_analysis']['yahoo_connection'] = cast_text[:500] detailed_analysis['key_findings'].append({ 'type': 'yahoo_connection', 'source': 'We Live in Public', 'details': cast_text[:300] }) # Look for production information and awards awards_section = soup.find(['h2', 'h3'], string=re.compile(r'Awards|Reception|Festival', re.IGNORECASE)) if awards_section: print(' Found Awards/Festival section') awards_content = awards_section.find_next_sibling() if awards_content: awards_text = awards_content.get_text() print(f' Awards info: {awards_text[:200]}...') if 'sundance' in awards_text.lower(): print(' 🏆 SUNDANCE CONNECTION CONFIRMED!') detailed_analysis['sundance_connections'].append({ 'film': 'We Live in Public', 'award_info': awards_text[:300] }) elif 'ondi_timoner' in html_file: print('\n🎥 ONDI TIMONER FILMOGRAPHY ANALYSIS:') # Look for filmography section filmography_section = soup.find(['h2', 'h3'], string=re.compile(r'Filmography|Films|Work|Career', re.IGNORECASE)) if filmography_section: print(' Found Filmography section') # Extract film list next_element = filmography_section.find_next_sibling() while next_element and next_element.name not in ['h1', 'h2']: if next_element.name in ['ul', 'ol']: films = next_element.find_all('li') for film in films: film_text = film.get_text().strip() if len(film_text) > 10: print(f' Film: {film_text}') # Check for Yahoo or tech connections film_lower = film_text.lower() if any(term in film_lower for term in ['yahoo', 'internet', 'tech', 'digital', 'online']): print(f' 🔍 Tech connection: {film_text}') detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography'].append({ 'title': film_text, 'tech_connection': True }) else: detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography'].append({ 'title': film_text, 'tech_connection': False }) next_element = next_element.find_next_sibling() elif 'imdb' in html_file: print('\n🎭 IMDB SEARCH RESULTS ANALYSIS:') # Look for search results result_elements = soup.find_all(['td', 'div', 'li'], class_=lambda x: x and any(term in str(x).lower() for term in ['result', 'title', 'findResult'])) print(f' Found {len(result_elements)} potential result elements') for i, element in enumerate(result_elements[:10], 1): element_text = element.get_text().strip() if len(element_text) > 20 and len(element_text) < 500: print(f' Result {i}: {element_text[:150]}...') element_lower = element_text.lower() if any(term in element_lower for term in ['jerry yang', 'yahoo', 'documentary']): print(f' ⭐ Relevant result found!') file_analysis['key_content'].append(element_text) detailed_analysis['files_analyzed'].append(file_analysis) except Exception as e: print(f'Error analyzing {html_file}: {str(e)}') continue print(f'Analysis complete for {html_file}') # Generate comprehensive summary print('\n' + '=' * 90) print('COMPREHENSIVE DOCUMENTARY CONNECTION ANALYSIS') print('=' * 90) print(f'\n📊 ANALYSIS SUMMARY:') print(f'Files analyzed: {len(detailed_analysis["files_analyzed"])}') print(f'Jerry Yang references found: {len(detailed_analysis["jerry_yang_references"])}') print(f'Documentary connections: {len(detailed_analysis["documentary_connections"])}') print(f'Sundance connections: {len(detailed_analysis["sundance_connections"])}') print(f'Ondi Timoner films cataloged: {len(detailed_analysis["ondi_timoner_filmography"])}') print(f'Key findings: {len(detailed_analysis["key_findings"])}') # Display key findings if detailed_analysis['key_findings']: print('\n🎯 KEY FINDINGS:') for i, finding in enumerate(detailed_analysis['key_findings'], 1): print(f'\n{i}. Type: {finding["type"]}') print(f' Source: {finding["source"]}') print(f' Details: {finding["details"][:200]}...') else: print('\n❌ No key documentary connections identified') # Analyze We Live in Public specifically if detailed_analysis['we_live_in_public_analysis']: print('\n🎬 WE LIVE IN PUBLIC DETAILED ANALYSIS:') for key, value in detailed_analysis['we_live_in_public_analysis'].items(): print(f' {key}: {value[:200]}...') else: print('\n🎬 No specific We Live in Public connections found') # Display Ondi Timoner filmography if detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography']: print('\n🎥 ONDI TIMONER FILMOGRAPHY:') tech_films = [f for f in detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography'] if f.get('tech_connection')] other_films = [f for f in detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography'] if not f.get('tech_connection')] if tech_films: print(f' Tech-related films ({len(tech_films)}):') for film in tech_films: print(f' - {film["title"]}') if other_films: print(f' Other films ({len(other_films)}):') for film in other_films[:5]: # Show first 5 print(f' - {film["title"]}') if len(other_films) > 5: print(f' ... and {len(other_films) - 5} more films') # Save detailed analysis analysis_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'jerry_yang_detailed_documentary_analysis.json') with open(analysis_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(detailed_analysis, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\n💾 DETAILED ANALYSIS SAVED TO: {analysis_file}') # Create final summary report summary_report = f""" 🎯 JERRY YANG DOCUMENTARY CONNECTION RESEARCH - FINAL REPORT RESEARCH OBJECTIVE: Identify Jerry Yang's appearances in documentaries, particularly connections to 'We Live in Public', Josh Harris, and Sundance Grand Jury Prize winners. METHODS USED: 1. Wikipedia page analysis (Jerry Yang, We Live in Public, Ondi Timoner) 2. IMDb search result analysis 3. Direct HTML content parsing and keyword extraction 4. Comprehensive text analysis for documentary references KEY FINDINGS: - Files analyzed: {len(detailed_analysis['files_analyzed'])} - Jerry Yang documentary references: {len(detailed_analysis['jerry_yang_references'])} - We Live in Public connections: {'Found' if detailed_analysis['we_live_in_public_analysis'] else 'None confirmed'} - Sundance connections: {len(detailed_analysis['sundance_connections'])} - Ondi Timoner films cataloged: {len(detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography'])} CONCLUSIONS: {'Specific documentary connections identified' if detailed_analysis['key_findings'] else 'No direct Jerry Yang documentary appearances confirmed through available sources'} RECOMMENDATIONS: 1. Review saved HTML files manually for missed connections 2. Search academic databases for tech documentary histories 3. Contact documentary filmmakers directly for cast/participant information 4. Check video streaming platforms for documentary credits Analysis completed: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')} """ print(summary_report) # Save summary report summary_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'jerry_yang_documentary_final_report.txt') with open(summary_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(summary_report) print(f'\n📄 FINAL SUMMARY REPORT SAVED TO: {summary_file}') print('\n🏁 COMPREHENSIVE JERRY YANG DOCUMENTARY ANALYSIS COMPLETE!') print('All source materials analyzed and findings documented for further research.')

Look for production information and awards awards_section = soup.find(['h2', 'h3'], string=re.compile(r'Awards|Reception|Festival', re.IGNORECASE)) if awards_section: print(' Found Awards/Festival section') awards_content = awards_section.find_next_sibling() if awards_content: awards_text = awards_content.get_text() print(f' Awards info: {awards_text[:200]}...') if 'sundance' in awards_text.lower(): print(' 🏆 SUNDANCE CONNECTION CONFIRMED!') detailed_analysis['sundance_connections'].append({ 'film': 'We Live in Public', 'award_info': awards_text[:300] }) elif 'ondi_timoner' in html_file: print('\n🎥 ONDI TIMONER FILMOGRAPHY ANALYSIS:') # Look for filmography section filmography_section = soup.find(['h2', 'h3'], string=re.compile(r'Filmography|Films|Work|Career', re.IGNORECASE)) if filmography_section: print(' Found Filmography section') # Extract film list next_element = filmography_section.find_next_sibling() while next_element and next_element.name not in ['h1', 'h2']: if next_element.name in ['ul', 'ol']: films = next_element.find_all('li') for film in films: film_text = film.get_text().strip() if len(film_text) > 10: print(f' Film: {film_text}') # Check for Yahoo or tech connections film_lower = film_text.lower() if any(term in film_lower for term in ['yahoo', 'internet', 'tech', 'digital', 'online']): print(f' 🔍 Tech connection: {film_text}') detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography'].append({ 'title': film_text, 'tech_connection': True }) else: detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography'].append({ 'title': film_text, 'tech_connection': False }) next_element = next_element.find_next_sibling() elif 'imdb' in html_file: print('\n🎭 IMDB SEARCH RESULTS ANALYSIS:') # Look for search results result_elements = soup.find_all(['td', 'div', 'li'], class_=lambda x: x and any(term in str(x).lower() for term in ['result', 'title', 'findResult'])) print(f' Found {len(result_elements)} potential result elements') for i, element in enumerate(result_elements[:10], 1): element_text = element.get_text().strip() if len(element_text) > 20 and len(element_text) < 500: print(f' Result {i}: {element_text[:150]}...') element_lower = element_text.lower() if any(term in element_lower for term in ['jerry yang', 'yahoo', 'documentary']): print(f' ⭐ Relevant result found!') file_analysis['key_content'].append(element_text) detailed_analysis['files_analyzed'].append(file_analysis) except Exception as e: print(f'Error analyzing {html_file}: {str(e)}') continue print(f'Analysis complete for {html_file}') # Type: {finding["type"]}') print(f' Source: {finding["source"]}') print(f' Details: {finding["details"][:200]}...') else: print('\n❌ No key documentary connections identified') # Analyze We Live in Public specifically if detailed_analysis['we_live_in_public_analysis']: print('\n🎬 WE LIVE IN PUBLIC DETAILED ANALYSIS:') for key, value in detailed_analysis['we_live_in_public_analysis'].items(): print(f' {key}: {value[:200]}...') else: print('\n🎬 No specific We Live in Public connections found') # Display Ondi Timoner filmography if detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography']: print('\n🎥 ONDI TIMONER FILMOGRAPHY:') tech_films = [f for f in detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography'] if f.get('tech_connection')] other_films = [f for f in detailed_analysis['ondi_timoner_filmography'] if not f.get('tech_connection')] if tech_films: print(f' Tech-related films ({len(tech_films)}):') for film in tech_films: print(f' - {film["title"]}') if other_films: print(f' Other films ({len(other_films)}):') for film in other_films[:5]: # Show first 5 print(f' - {film["title"]}') if len(other_films) > 5: print(f' ... and {len(other_films) - 5} more films') # Save detailed analysis analysis_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'jerry_yang_detailed_documentary_analysis.json') with open(analysis_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(detailed_analysis, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\n💾 DETAILED ANALYSIS SAVED TO: {analysis_file}') # Create final summary report summary_report = f""" 🎯 JERRY YANG DOCUMENTARY CONNECTION RESEARCH - FINAL REPORT RESEARCH OBJECTIVE: Identify Jerry Yang's appearances in documentaries, particularly connections to 'We Live in Public', Josh Harris, and Sundance Grand Jury Prize winners.
